Each IP makes 2 requests (at limit)\n        for ip in ips:\n            for i in range(2):\n                request = self.rf.get('/', REMOTE_ADDR=ip)\n                response = middleware.process_request(request)\n                self.assertIsNone(response)\n\n        # Each IP tries 1 more request (should be blocked)\n        for ip in ips:\n            request = self.rf.get('/', REMOTE_ADDR=ip)\n            response = middleware.process_request(request)\n            self.assertEqual(response.status_code, 429, f\"IP {ip} should be rate limited\")\n\n    @override_settings(RATE_LIMIT_REQUESTS=1, RATE_LIMIT_WINDOW=3600)\n    def test_single_request_limit(self):\n        \"\"\"Test with limit set to 1 request.\"\"\"\n        middleware = RateLimitMiddleware(get_response)\n\n        #
